Additionally, could you incorporate any necessary alerts?                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |

Additionally, {HE/SHE} has expressed a preference for {CARDIO/STRENGTH/FLEXIBILITY} workouts and possesses a {BEGINNER/INTERMEDIATE/ADVANCED} fitness level. It would be greatly appreciated if you could incorporate both {EQUIPMENT/NO EQUIPMENT} exercises into the plan.                                                                                                                                                        |
